The child was sick and was transferred to Fuwai, but he was afraid of taking it home for fear of danger at any time, so he stayed at the Metropark Hotel, which is close to Fuwai Hospital and has a nice environment. When he checked in, the front desk learned about the situation and was very attentive in arranging for colleagues on the same floor. Pay attention, and also carefully arrange to prepare extra quilts, sheets and purifiers. The next morning, I took my child to the hospital and didn't have time to check out. The child's condition was special and he couldn't leave the hospital. Seeing that the check-out time was approaching and he couldn't make it back to the hotel in time, he called the front desk to pay attention and make proper arrangements. From check-in to check-out, the Metropark staff I encountered were warm-spoken, patient and meticulous, which made me feel confident after being depressed and anxious for 16 days. Thank you Weijing! Thank you to every staff member I met at Metropark! !
After checking in, the child liked the hotel room decoration and design very much. It was clean and sunny, and he would stay at Metropark for a few more days after being discharged from the hospital.
